<p><b>Hakim Ziyech</b> (<small>Dutch pronunciation:&#32;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Dutch" title="Help:IPA/Dutch">[zij]</a></span>; <a href="/wiki/Berber_languages" title="Berber languages">Berber</a>:  , <a href="/wiki/Arabic_language" class="mw-redirect" title="Arabic language">Arabic</a>: <span lang="ar" dir="rtl"> </span>&#8206;; born 19 March 1993) is a professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as an <a href="/wiki/Attacking_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Attacking midfielder">attacking midfielder</a> or <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Winger" title="Midfielder">winger</a> for <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Morocco_national_football_team" title="Morocco national football team">Morocco national team</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He is known for his finishing, <a href="/wiki/Dribbling#Association_football" title="Dribbling">dribbling</a>, long passes, technique, and ability from <a href="/wiki/Direct_free_kick" class="mw-redirect" title="Direct free kick">free kicks</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> In 2019, he was selected as one of the 20 best players in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League#Squad_of_the_season" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League">2018–19 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-auto_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> At the end of the same year, he was ranked 29th in <a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a>'s list of "The 100 best footballers in the world".<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ziyech started his professional career at Dutch club <a href="/wiki/SC_Heerenveen" title="SC Heerenveen">Heerenveen</a> in 2012 and signed for fellow Dutch club <a href="/wiki/FC_Twente" title="FC Twente">Twente</a> two years later.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:1_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> In 2016 he signed for Ajax on a five-year deal, with a reported transfer fee of €11m.<sup id="cite_ref-:3_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:3-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:4_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:4-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> The <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Eredivisie" title="2018–19 Eredivisie">2018–19</a> season was the most prolific season in Ziyech's career, as he scored 16 goals and provided 13 assists in the Eredivisie.<sup id="cite_ref-:2_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> He joined Premier League club Chelsea for the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_Chelsea_F.C._season" title="2020–21 Chelsea F.C. season">2020–21 season</a>.
</p><p>Originally eligible to play for the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_football_team" title="Netherlands national football team">Netherlands</a> or <a href="/wiki/Morocco_national_football_team" title="Morocco national football team">Morocco</a> at international level,<sup id="cite_ref-Football_Oranje_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Football_Oranje-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> he has represented Morocco<sup id="cite_ref-:5_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:5-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:6_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:6-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> at the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> and the <a href="/wiki/2019_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2019 Africa Cup of Nations">2019 Africa Cup of Nations</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-:7_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:7-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:8_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:8-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hakim_Ziyech&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Heerenveen">Heerenveen</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hakim_Ziyech&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Heerenveen">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Ziyech was born in <a href="/wiki/Dronten" title="Dronten">Dronten</a> in the Netherlands. Between 2001 and 2007, he played for the youth academy of Reaal Dronten and ASV Dronten. In 2007, he joined the Heerenveen academy.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 2 August 2012, Ziyech made his formal debut for <a href="/wiki/SC_Heerenveen" title="SC Heerenveen">Heerenveen</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_UEFA_Europa_League_qualifying_phase_and_play-off_round#Heerenveen_v_Rapid_Bucureti" class="mw-redirect" title="2012–13 UEFA Europa League qualifying phase and play-off round">first leg</a> of the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_UEFA_Europa_League_qualifying_phase_and_play-off_round#Third_qualifying_round" class="mw-redirect" title="2012–13 UEFA Europa League qualifying phase and play-off round">third qualifying round</a> of the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_UEFA_Europa_League" title="2012–13 UEFA Europa League">Europa League</a>, against <a href="/wiki/FC_Rapid_Bucure%C8%99ti" title="FC Rapid Bucureti">Rapid Bucureti</a>, playing a total of 53 minutes before being substituted.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> He made his <a href="/wiki/Eredivisie" title="Eredivisie">Eredivisie</a> debut for the club on 10 August, in a 0–2 loss to <a href="/wiki/N.E.C._(football_club)" class="mw-redirect" title="N.E.C. (football club)">NEC</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> Ziyech scored his first goal for Heerenveen in a 2–0 win over <a href="/wiki/NAC_Breda" title="NAC Breda">NAC Breda</a>, on 10 August 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> On 23 August, Ziyech provided two assists in a 3–3 draw with <a href="/wiki/AFC_Ajax" title="AFC Ajax">Ajax</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> On 8 November, Ziyech scored and provided an assist in a 5–2 win over <a href="/wiki/RKC_Waalwijk" title="RKC Waalwijk">Waalwijk</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> On 18 December, Ziyech scored two goals against <a href="/wiki/AZ_Alkmaar" title="AZ Alkmaar">AZ Alkmaar</a>, in the fourth round of the KNVB Cup, one in regular time and a last-minute penalty to draw level and take the game into a penalty shootout, but he missed his penalty and Heerenveen were knocked out 6–5 on penalties.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> On 21 December, Ziyech scored twice and provided one assist in a 5–1 away win over <a href="/wiki/AZ_Alkmaar" title="AZ Alkmaar">AZ Alkmaar</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> On 18 January 2014, Ziyech scored in a 2–2 draw with <a href="/wiki/Roda_JC_Kerkrade" title="Roda JC Kerkrade">Roda</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> On 9 February, he scored in a 3–1 win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Groningen" title="FC Groningen">Groningen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> On 27 April, Ziyech scored once and provided an assist in a 4–1 win over Utrecht, after coming on as a substitute.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Twente">Twente</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hakim_Ziyech&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Twente">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On 18 August 2014, Ziyech joined <a href="/wiki/FC_Twente" title="FC Twente">Twente</a> for €3.5m, signing on a three-year contract and taking the number 10 shirt.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:9_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:9-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> On 5 October, Ziyech scored once and provided an assist in a 2–2 draw with <a href="/wiki/AZ_Alkmaar" title="AZ Alkmaar">AZ Alkmaar</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> On 6 March 2015, Ziyech scored twice in a 2–2 draw with <a href="/wiki/Willem_II_(football_club)" title="Willem II (football club)">Willem II</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> On 10 May, he provided three assists in a 3–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Dordrecht" title="FC Dordrecht">Dordrecht</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> On 17 May, Ziyech scored twice and provided an assist in a 3–1 away win over his former club <a href="/wiki/Heerenveen_S.C." class="mw-redirect" title="Heerenveen S.C.">Heerenveen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> Ziyech finished the season with 11 goals and 15 assists in the Eredivisie.<sup id="cite_ref-:9_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:9-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> For the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_FC_Twente_season" title="2015–16 FC Twente season">2015–16 season</a>, Ziyech was selected as captain of the club; however, he was stripped of the captaincy in early January 2016, after he made disrespectful comments against the club and publicly requesting a transfer.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> The 2015–16 season was the most prolific season in Ziyech's career, as he scored 17 goals and provided 10 assist in the Eredivisie.<sup id="cite_ref-:2_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ajax">Ajax</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hakim_Ziyech&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Ajax">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.932018:_Initial_seasons_and_European_final"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–2018:_Initial_seasons_and_European_final">2016–2018: Initial seasons and European final</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hakim_Ziyech&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: 2016–2018: Initial seasons and European final">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 30 August 2016, Ziyech signed for <a href="/wiki/AFC_Ajax" title="AFC Ajax">Ajax</a> on a five-year deal, with a reported transfer of €11m.<sup id="cite_ref-:3_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:3-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:4_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:4-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> On 15 September, Ziyech was given a red card in the 79th minute, in a 2–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Panathinaikos_F.C." title="Panathinaikos F.C.">Panathinaikos</a> in the opening group game of the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Europa_League_group_stage#Group_G" title="2016–17 UEFA Europa League group stage">Europa League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Six days later, on 21 September, he scored his first goal for Ajax in a 5–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Willem_II_(football_club)" title="Willem II (football club)">Willem II</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_KNVB_Cup#First_round" title="2016–17 KNVB Cup">KNVB Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> On 2 October, Ziyech scored his first league goal for the club in a 3–2 win over Utrecht.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> On 20 October, he scored in a 2–2 draw with <a href="/wiki/RC_Celta_de_Vigo" title="RC Celta de Vigo">Celta Vigo</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Europa_League_group_stage#Group_G" title="2016–17 UEFA Europa League group stage">Europa League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> On 20 October, he scored in a 1–0 win over <a href="/wiki/S.B.V._Excelsior" class="mw-redirect" title="S.B.V. Excelsior">Excelsior</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> On 3 November, Ziyech scored in the reverse fixture against Celta Vigo in the Europa League, a 3–2 win.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> On 4 December, he scored a penalty in a 2–0 win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Groningen" title="FC Groningen">Groningen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> On 15 January 2017, Ziyech scored twice in a 3–1 away win over <a href="/wiki/PEC_Zwolle" title="PEC Zwolle">Zwolle</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> On 29 January, he scored in a 3–0 win over <a href="/wiki/ADO_Den_Haag" title="ADO Den Haag">Den Haag</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> On 8 April, he scored in a 5–1 away win over <a href="/wiki/N.E.C._(football_club)" class="mw-redirect" title="N.E.C. (football club)">NEC</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 12 August 2017, Ziyech scored the opening goal in a 1–2 defeat to <a href="/wiki/Heracles_Almelo" title="Heracles Almelo">Heracles Almelo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> On 20 August, Ziyech scored in a 3–1 win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Groningen" title="FC Groningen">Groningen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> On 9 September, Ziyech missed a penalty but eventually scored just five minutes later in a 3–0 win over <a href="/wiki/PEC_Zwolle" title="PEC Zwolle">Zwolle</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> On 18 November, Ziyech provided an assist in an 8–0 win over NAC Breda.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> On 26 November, he provided an assist in a 5–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Roda_JC_Kerkrade" title="Roda JC Kerkrade">Roda</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> On 14 December, Ziyech scored in a 3–1 win over Excelsior.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> On 20 December, Ziyech missed a penalty against his former club <a href="/wiki/FC_Twente" title="FC Twente">Twente</a>, in the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_KNVB_Cup#Round_of_16" title="2017–18 KNVB Cup">round of sixteen</a> of the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_KNVB_Cup" title="2017–18 KNVB Cup">KNVB Cup</a>, with Ajax suffering elimination after losing the <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shoot-out_(association_football)" title="Penalty shoot-out (association football)">penalty shootout</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> On 4 February 2018, Ziyech scored an injury-time goal in a 3–1 win over <a href="/wiki/NAC_Breda" title="NAC Breda">NAC Breda</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, on 7 February, he scored in a 4–2 away win over Roda.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> On 18 March, Ziyech scored twice in a 5–2 away win over <a href="/wiki/Sparta_Rotterdam" title="Sparta Rotterdam">Sparta Rotterdam</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> On 19 April, Ziyech scored in a 4–1 win over <a href="/wiki/VVV-Venlo" title="VVV-Venlo">Venlo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.932020:_Domestic_double_and_departure"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–2020:_Domestic_double_and_departure">2018–2020: Domestic double and departure</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hakim_Ziyech&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 2018–2020: Domestic double and departure">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 25 July 2018, Ziyech scored in a <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League_qualifying_phase_and_play-off_round#Q2_L2.1" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League qualifying phase and play-off round">2–0</a> win over <a href="/wiki/SK_Sturm_Graz" title="SK Sturm Graz">Sturm Graz</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League_qualifying_phase_and_play-off_round#Second_qualifying_round" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League qualifying phase and play-off round">second qualifying round</a> of the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> On 22 August 2018, Ziyech scored in a <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League_qualifying_phase_and_play-off_round#PO_L2.1" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League qualifying phase and play-off round">3–1</a> win over Dynamo Kyiv in the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League_qualifying_phase_and_play-off_round#Play-off_round" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League qualifying phase and play-off round">play-off round</a> of the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> On 13 February 2019, he scored his first Champions League goal, scoring the equaliser in a 1–2 loss against <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a> in the round of 16.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> On 5 March 2019, he scored again in the 4–1 victory over Real Madrid in the second leg, which saw the title holders being knocked out and bringing Ajax to the quarter-finals, where they eliminated <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a> to reach the semi–finals of the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 30 April 2019, Ziyech assisted for the only goal in the Champions League semi–final first leg win at <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> He also scored the second goal for Ajax in the second leg of the semi-final, where Ajax were beaten 3–2 by Tottenham and were knocked out of the tournament on away goals with a 3–3 aggregate score.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> In August 2019, he signed a new three-year contract with Ajax.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="2019–20 UEFA Champions League group stage">2019–20 UEFA Champions League group stage</a>, Ziyech scored one goal each in a 3–0 away win against <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> and in a 2–0 away win over <a href="/wiki/Lille_OSC" title="Lille OSC">Lille</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> However, Ajax lost 1–0 at home to Valencia to be eliminated at the group stage.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Chelsea">Chelsea</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hakim_Ziyech&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Chelsea">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21_season">2020–21 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hakim_Ziyech&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 2020–21 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 14 February 2020, it was announced that Ajax and <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> had reached an agreement for the transfer of Ziyech for a fee of €40&#160;million (potentially increasing to a maximum of €44&#160;million, with variable factors). He joined the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club for the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_Chelsea_F.C._season" title="2020–21 Chelsea F.C. season">2020–21 season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> Ten days later, Chelsea announced they had agreed personal terms with Ziyech and that he had signed a five-year contract.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> Ziyech made his league debut for Chelsea on 17 October 2020, in a 3–3 home draw against <a href="/wiki/Southampton_F.C." title="Southampton F.C.">Southampton</a> after he came off from the bench.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> On 28 October 2020, he scored his first Chelsea goal in a 4–0 away win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Krasnodar" title="FC Krasnodar">Krasnodar</a> on matchday two of the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2020–21 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, Ziyech started his first league match for Chelsea, contributing with a goal and an assist in a 3–0 away win over <a href="/wiki/Burnley_F.C." title="Burnley F.C.">Burnley</a>. In doing so, Ziyech became the first Chelsea player since <a href="/wiki/Diego_Costa" title="Diego Costa">Diego Costa</a> to score in his first two starts for Chelsea in all competitions.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> In Chelsea's next league match, Ziyech provided two assists and was named the man of the match as Chelsea defeated <a href="/wiki/Sheffield_United_F.C." title="Sheffield United F.C.">Sheffield United</a> by a score of 4–1.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hakim_Ziyech&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Netherlands">Netherlands</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hakim_Ziyech&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Netherlands">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Ziyech was originally eligible to play for the national teams of the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_football_team" title="Netherlands national football team">Netherlands</a>, where he was born and raised, or the land of his heritage, <a href="/wiki/Morocco_national_football_team" title="Morocco national football team">Morocco</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Football_Oranje_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Football_Oranje-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> He played for Dutch national youth teams, playing for the U19s, U20s and <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_under-21_football_team" title="Netherlands national under-21 football team">U21s</a>. He received his first call-up to the senior squad in May 2015, for friendly matches against the <a href="/wiki/United_States_men%27s_national_soccer_team" title="United States men&#39;s national soccer team">United States</a> and <a href="/wiki/Latvia_national_football_team" title="Latvia national football team">Latvia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Football_Oranje_13-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Football_Oranje-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Morocco">Morocco</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hakim_Ziyech&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Morocco">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:157px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Iran-Morocco_by_soccer.ru_14_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/a/aa/Iran-Morocco_by_soccer.ru_14_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="155" height="276" class="thumbimage" data-file-width="155" data-file-height="276" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Iran-Morocco_by_soccer.ru_14_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Ziyech with <a href="/wiki/Morocco_national_football_team" title="Morocco national football team">Morocco</a> in 2018</div></div></div>
<p>In September 2015, Ziyech confirmed his choice to represent Morocco on the international stage.<sup id="cite_ref-:5_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:5-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:6_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:6-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Ziyech made his debut for the national team on 9 October, in a 1–0 defeat to the <a href="/wiki/Ivory_Coast_national_football_team" title="Ivory Coast national football team">Ivory Coast</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> On 27 May 2016, he scored his first two goals for Morocco, in a 2–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Congo_national_football_team" title="Congo national football team">Congo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> On 4 September, Ziyech scored in a 2–0 win over <a href="/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe_national_football_team" title="São Tomé and Príncipe national football team">São Tomé and Príncipe</a> in a <a href="/wiki/2017_Africa_Cup_of_Nations_qualification" title="2017 Africa Cup of Nations qualification">2017 Africa Cup of Nations qualifying</a> match.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> Ziyech was not selected for <a href="/wiki/2017_Africa_Cup_of_Nations_squads#Morocco" title="2017 Africa Cup of Nations squads">the final 23-man squad</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2017_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2017 Africa Cup of Nations">2017 Africa Cup of Nations</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 1 September 2017, Ziyech scored in a 6–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Mali_national_football_team" title="Mali national football team">Mali</a>, in a <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_CAF_Third_Round" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – CAF Third Round">qualifying match</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> He was selected for the final <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_squads#Morocco" title="2018 FIFA World Cup squads">23-man squad</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-:7_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:7-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:8_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:8-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hakim_Ziyech&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Honours">Honours</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Hakim_Ziyech&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Honours">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Eredivisie" title="Eredivisie">Eredivisie</a>: <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Eredivisie" title="2018–19 Eredivisie">2018–19</a></li>
